    <script>
      // Mobile menu toggle
      const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
      const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
      const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
      const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
      const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

      mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
        // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
        if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
        } else {
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
        }
      });

      mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
      });

      // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
      const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
      mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
        link.addEventListener('click', () => {
          mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
        });
      });
    </script>

    <!-- Floating Scroll to Top Button -->
    <button
      id="scroll-to-top"
      class="hidden fixed bottom-8 right-8 text-white p-2 rounded-full shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition-all duration-300 z-50"
      style="background-color: #ffffff; color: #004900;"

    <script>
      let lastScrollTop = 0;
      const banner = document.getElementById("top-banner");
      const nav = document.getElementById("main-nav");
      const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById("scroll-to-top");
      const floatingCta = document.getElementById("floating-cta");

      window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
        let scrollTop =
          window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

        // Hide/Show banner on scroll
        if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
          banner.style.transform = "translateY(-100%)";
          nav.style.top = "0";
        } else {
          banner.style.transform = "translateY(0)";
          nav.style.top = "36px";
        }

        lastScrollTop = scrollTop;

        // Show/Hide scroll to top & CTA
        if (scrollTop > 300) {
          scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove("hidden");
          floatingCta.classList.remove("hidden");
        } else {
          scrollToTopBtn.classList.add("hidden");
          floatingCta.classList.add("hidden");
        }
      });

      // Scroll to top functionality
      scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        window.scrollTo({
          top: 0,
          behavior: "smooth",
        });
      });
    </script>

    <script>
      // Mobile menu toggle
      const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
      const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
      const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
      const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
      const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

      mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
        // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
        if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
        } else {
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
        }
      });

      mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
      });

      // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
      const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
      mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
        link.addEventListener('click', () => {
          mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
          menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
          menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
        });
      });
    </script>

<!-- Slider Script (Vanilla JS) -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll(".slider-slide");
    const thumbs = document.querySelectorAll(".thumb-btn");
    const prevBtn = document.getElementById("sliderPrev");
    const nextBtn = document.getElementById("sliderNext");
    const captionEl = document.getElementById("sliderCaption");

    const captions = [
      "Underground installation – compact, space-saving design.",
      "Heavy-duty FRP body – leak-proof and corrosion-resistant.",
      "Odour-free outlet – clean surroundings even after years.",
      "Quick and neat installation by trained technicians."
    ];

    let current = 0;

    function showSlide(index) {
      slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
        if (i === index) {
          slide.style.opacity = "1";
          slide.style.transform = "scale(1)";
          slide.style.zIndex = "10";
        } else {
          slide.style.opacity = "0";
          slide.style.transform = "scale(0.95)";
          slide.style.zIndex = "0";
        }
      });

      thumbs.forEach((thumb, i) => {
        if (i === index) {
          thumb.classList.add("border-emerald-500");
          thumb.classList.remove("border-transparent");
        } else {
          thumb.classList.remove("border-emerald-500");
          thumb.classList.add("border-transparent");
        }
      });

      if (captionEl) {
        captionEl.textContent = captions[index] || "";
      }

      current = index;
    }

    function nextSlide() {
      let next = current + 1;
      if (next >= slides.length) next = 0;
      showSlide(next);
    }

    function prevSlide() {
      let prev = current - 1;
      if (prev < 0) prev = slides.length - 1;
      showSlide(prev);
    }

    // Event listeners
    if (nextBtn) nextBtn.addEventListener("click", nextSlide);
    if (prevBtn) prevBtn.addEventListener("click", prevSlide);

    thumbs.forEach((thumb) => {
      thumb.addEventListener("click", () => {
        const index = parseInt(thumb.getAttribute("data-slide"), 10);
        showSlide(index);
      });
    });

    // Auto-play (optional – comment this block if you don’t want auto-slide)
    let autoPlay = setInterval(nextSlide, 6000);

    // Pause on hover
    const sliderArea = document.getElementById("sliderTrack")?.parentElement;
    if (sliderArea) {
      sliderArea.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => clearInterval(autoPlay));
      sliderArea.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => {
        autoPlay = setInterval(nextSlide, 6000);
      });
    }

    // Init
    showSlide(0);
  });
</script>


  <section class="py-20 bg-gray-50">
  <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
      
    <!-- Heading -->
    <div class="text-center mb-12">
      <h2 class="text-4xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">
        FRP Bio-Septic Tank Installation Layout
      </h2>
      <p class="text-lg text-gray-600 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
        A simple, clear explanation of how the FRP Bio-Septic Tank is installed at your site — 
        showing the toilet line, screen chamber, FRP tank, and soak pit connection.
      </p>

      class="hidden fixed bottom-8 right-8 text-white p-4 rounded-full shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition-all duration-300 z-50"
      style="background-color: #ffffff; color: #004900;"

    <script>
      let lastScrollTop = 0;
      const banner = document.getElementById("top-banner");
      const nav = document.getElementById("main-nav");
      const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById("scroll-to-top");
      const floatingCta = document.getElementById("floating-cta");

      window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
        let scrollTop =
          window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

        // Hide/Show banner on scroll
        if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
          // Scrolling down
          banner.style.transform = "translateY(-100%)";
          nav.style.top = "0";
        } else {
          // Scrolling up
          banner.style.transform = "translateY(0)";
          nav.style.top = "36px";
        }

        lastScrollTop = scrollTop;

        // Show/Hide scroll to top button
        if (scrollTop > 300) {
          scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove("hidden");
          floatingCta.classList.remove("hidden");
        } else {
          scrollToTopBtn.classList.add("hidden");
          floatingCta.classList.add("hidden");
        }
      });

      // Scroll to top functionality
      scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        window.scrollTo({
          top: 0,
          behavior: "smooth",
        });
      });
    </script>

          <!-- script for Contact Form Card -->
           <script>
              document.getElementById("submitBtn").addEventListener("click", function () {

                const templateParams = {
                  name: document.getElementById("name").value,
                  phone: document.getElementById("phone").value,
                  email: document.getElementById("email").value,
                  location: document.getElementById("location").value,
                  property_type: document.getElementById("property_type").value,
                  users: document.getElementById("users").value,
                  message: document.getElementById("message").value
                };

                // basic validation
                if (!templateParams.name || !templateParams.phone) {
                  alert("Please fill required fields.");
                  return;
                }

                emailjs.send(
                  "service_pioneer",
                  "template_biotank",
                  templateParams
                ).then(
                  function () {
                    alert("Thank you! We will contact you within 24 hours.");

                    // optional reset
                    Object.keys(templateParams).forEach(id => {
                      const el = document.getElementById(id);
                      if (el) el.value = "";
                    });
                  },
                  function (error) {
                    alert("Failed to send. Please try again.");
                    console.error("EmailJS Error:", error);
                  }
                );
              });
            </script>
<!-- End Contact Form Card -->

  <!-- Mobile menu JS -->
  <script>
    const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
    const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
    const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
    const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
    const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

    mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
      // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
      if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      } else {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
      }
    });

    mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
    });

    // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
    const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
    mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      });
    });
  </script>

  <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    
    <div class="grid md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-[1.05fr_1.2fr] gap-6 sm:gap-8 md:gap-12 items-center pt-8 sm:pt-12 md:pt-16 pb-10 sm:pb-16 md:pb-20">

    <script>
        let lastScrollTop = 0;
        const banner = document.getElementById('top-banner');
        const nav = document.getElementById('main-nav');
        const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-to-top');
        const floatingCta = document.getElementById('floating-cta');
        
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            let scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
            
            // Hide/Show banner on scroll
            if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
                // Scrolling down
                banner.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
                nav.style.top = '0';
            } else {
                // Scrolling up
                banner.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                nav.style.top = '36px'';
            }
            
            lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
            
            // Show/Hide scroll to top button
            if (scrollTop > 300) {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
                floatingCta.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('hidden');
                floatingCta.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        });
        
        // Scroll to top functionality
        scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({
                top: 0,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
  const cards = document.querySelectorAll(".stat-card");

  cards.forEach(card => {
    card.addEventListener("click", () => {
      cards.forEach(c => {
        c.classList.remove("bg-[#004900]", "text-white", "scale-105");
      });

      card.classList.add("bg-[#004900]", "text-white", "scale-105");
    });
  });
</script>



<!-- VIDEO & STAT CARDS ANIMATION SCRIPT -->
<script>
  // Video controls
  const video = document.getElementById("heroVideo");
  const btn = document.getElementById("videoBtn");
  const playIcon = document.getElementById("playIcon");
  const pauseIcon = document.getElementById("pauseIcon");

  btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (video.paused) {
      video.play();
      playIcon.classList.add("hidden");
      pauseIcon.classList.remove("hidden");
    } else {
      video.pause();
      playIcon.classList.remove("hidden");
      pauseIcon.classList.add("hidden");
    }
  });

  // Stat cards automatic color cycling
  const statCards = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-card');
  let currentActiveIndex = 0;

  function updateCardStyles() {
    statCards.forEach((card, index) => {
      // Remove all possible classes
      card.classList.remove(
        'bg-[#004900]', 'bg-white',
        'text-white', 'text-[#004900]'
      );

      if (index === currentActiveIndex) {
        // Active card (green background with white text)
        card.classList.add('bg-[#004900]', 'text-white');
      } else {
        // Inactive cards (white background with green text)
        card.classList.add('bg-white', 'text-[#004900]');
      }
    });

    // Move to next card
    currentActiveIndex = (currentActiveIndex + 1) % statCards.length;
  }

  // Initialize first card as active
  updateCardStyles();

  // Cycle every 2 seconds
  setInterval(updateCardStyles, 2000);
</script>


<!-- YouTube API + Hero Controls -->
<script>
  let player;
  let hideTimeout;

  function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
    player = new YT.Player('ytplayer', {});
  }

  // Load YouTube Player API
  const ytTag = document.createElement('script');
  ytTag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
  document.body.appendChild(ytTag);

  const btn = document.getElementById("videoToggle");
  const icon = document.getElementById("toggleIcon");
  const hero = document.getElementById("heroSection");

  // Play/pause toggle
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (player && player.getPlayerState() === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING) {
      player.pauseVideo();
      icon.classList.remove("fa-pause");
      icon.classList.add("fa-play");
    } else if (player) {
      player.playVideo();
      icon.classList.remove("fa-play");
      icon.classList.add("fa-pause");
    }
  });

  // Auto hide play/pause button
  function hideButton() {
    btn.classList.add("opacity-0");
  }

  function showButton() {
    btn.classList.remove("opacity-0");
    clearTimeout(hideTimeout);
    hideTimeout = setTimeout(hideButton, 3000);
  }

  hero.addEventListener("mousemove", showButton);
  hero.addEventListener("touchstart", showButton);
  hideTimeout = setTimeout(hideButton, 3000);
</script>

<!-- JS: click card → scroll to form & pre-fill field -->
<script>
  // Change this to your actual form id
  const form = document.querySelector("#contact-form");
  // Optional: a hidden/input field where we store selected type
  const homeTypeField = document.querySelector("#homeTypeField");

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-home-type]").forEach((card) => {
    card.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const value = card.getAttribute("data-home-type");

      if (homeTypeField) {
        // for input/select/textarea
        homeTypeField.value = value;
      }

      if (form) {
        form.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
      }
    });
  });
</script>

<!-- Optional: simple counter animation -->
<script>
  const counters = document.querySelectorAll('#installed-south-india .counter');
  let countersStarted = false;

  function animateCounters() {
    if (countersStarted) return;
    countersStarted = true;

    counters.forEach(counter => {
      const target = parseInt(counter.getAttribute('data-target'), 10);
      let current = 0;
      const duration = 1200;
      const startTime = performance.now();

      function update(now) {
        const progress = Math.min((now - startTime) / duration, 1);
        current = Math.floor(progress * target);
        counter.textContent = current.toLocaleString('en-IN');
        if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(update);
        else counter.textContent = target.toLocaleString('en-IN');
      }

      requestAnimationFrame(update);
    });
  }

  const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
    entries => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
          animateCounters();
          observer.disconnect();
        }
      });
    },
    { threshold: 0.3 }
  );

  const section = document.querySelector('#installed-south-india');
  if (section) observer.observe(section);
</script>





<!-- JS for Gallery + FAQ -->
<script>
  /* --- GALLERY SLIDER --- */
  const track = document.getElementById('galleryTrack');
  const slider = document.getElementById('gallerySlider');
  const slides = track.children.length;
  let index = 0;

  document.getElementById('nextBtn').onclick = () => {
    index = (index + 1) % slides;
    track.style.transform = `translateX(-${index * 100}%)`;
  };
  document.getElementById('prevBtn').onclick = () => {
    index = (index - 1 + slides) % slides;
    track.style.transform = `translateX(-${index * 100}%)`;
  };

  /* --- FAQ ACCORDION --- */
  document.querySelectorAll('.faq-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const content = btn.nextElementSibling;
      const icon = btn.querySelector('i');

      if (content.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        content.classList.remove('hidden');
        icon.classList.replace('fa-plus', 'fa-minus');
      } else {
        content.classList.add('hidden');
        icon.classList.replace('fa-minus', 'fa-plus');
      }
    });
  });
</script>

<script>
  // WhatsApp link handler (optional - for thank you page)
  const whatsappLink = document.getElementById("whatsapp-link");
  const thankyouWrapper = document.getElementById("thankyou-wrapper");

  // Build WhatsApp message when showing thank you (can be called from script.js)
  window.buildWhatsAppLink = function(formData) {
    const msgLines = [
      "Hi, I submitted the form on your website for a Bio-Septic tank.",
      "",
      formData.name && `Name: ${formData.name}`,
      formData.mobile && `Mobile: ${formData.mobile}`,
      formData.location && `Location: ${formData.location}`,
      formData.type && `Type: ${formData.type}`,
      formData.people && `No. of people: ${formData.people}`,
      formData.home_type && `Home type selection: ${formData.home_type}`,
      formData.preferred_contact && `Preferred contact: ${formData.preferred_contact}`,
    ].filter(Boolean);

    const text = encodeURIComponent(msgLines.join("\n"));
    const whatsappNumber = "919876543210";
    const waUrl = `https://wa.me/${whatsappNumber}?text=${text}`;
    
    if (whatsappLink) {
      whatsappLink.href = waUrl;
    }

    // Auto-open WhatsApp if preferred
    if (formData.preferred_contact === "WhatsApp") {
      window.open(waUrl, "_blank");
    }
  };
</script>

  <!-- YouTube API + Hero Controls -->
  <script>
    let player;
    let hideTimeout;

    function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
      player = new YT.Player('ytplayer', {});
    }

    // Load YouTube Player API
    const ytTag = document.createElement('script');
    ytTag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
    document.body.appendChild(ytTag);

    const btn = document.getElementById("videoToggle");
    const icon = document.getElementById("toggleIcon");
    const hero = document.getElementById("heroSection");

    // Play/pause toggle
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      if (player && player.getPlayerState() === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING) {
        player.pauseVideo();
        icon.classList.remove("fa-pause");
        icon.classList.add("fa-play");
      } else if (player) {
        player.playVideo();
        icon.classList.remove("fa-play");
        icon.classList.add("fa-pause");
      }
    });

    // Auto hide play/pause button
    function hideButton() {
      btn.classList.add("opacity-0");
    }

    function showButton() {
      btn.classList.remove("opacity-0");
      clearTimeout(hideTimeout);
      hideTimeout = setTimeout(hideButton, 3000);
    }

    hero.addEventListener("mousemove", showButton);
    hero.addEventListener("touchstart", showButton);
    hideTimeout = setTimeout(hideButton, 3000);
  </script>

  <!-- Navbar + Scroll to Top behaviour -->
  <script>
    // Mobile menu toggle
    const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
    const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
    const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
    const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
    const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

    mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
      // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
      if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      } else {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
      }
    });

    mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
    });

    // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
    const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
    mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      });
    });

    // Banner + Navbar + Scroll to top logic
    let lastScrollTop = 0;
    const banner = document.getElementById('top-banner');
    const nav = document.getElementById('main-nav');
    const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-to-top');

    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      let scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

      // Hide/Show banner and adjust navbar position
      if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
        // Scrolling down
        banner.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
        nav.style.top = '0';
      } else {
        // Scrolling up
        banner.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
        nav.style.top = '36px'';
      }
      lastScrollTop = scrollTop;

      // Show/Hide scroll to top button
      if (scrollTop > 300) {
        scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
      } else {
        scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('hidden');
      }
    });

    scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
    });

    // Mobile menu toggle (duplicate section removed - see earlier in script)
  </script>

  <script>
    // Mobile menu toggle
    const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
    const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
    const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
    const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
    const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

    mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
      // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
      if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      } else {
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
      }
    });

    mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
    });

    // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
    const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
    mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
        menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
        menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
      });
    });
  </script>

<script>
  // Tabs: Residential / Commercial
  const tabButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');
  const tabPanels = document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab-panel]');

  tabButtons.forEach((btn) => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const target = btn.getAttribute('data-tab-target');

      // Update button styles
      tabButtons.forEach((b) => {
        b.classList.remove('bg-emerald-500', 'text-white', 'font-semibold');
        b.classList.add('text-slate-700');
      });
      btn.classList.add('bg-emerald-500', 'text-white', 'font-semibold');
      btn.classList.remove('text-slate-700');

      // Show correct panel
      tabPanels.forEach((panel) => {
        if (panel.getAttribute('data-tab-panel') === target) {
          panel.classList.remove('hidden');
        } else {
          panel.classList.add('hidden');
        }
      });
    });
  });
</script>

    id="floating-cta"
    class="hidden fixed bottom-24 right-8 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-full shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition-all duration-300 z-50 font-semibold"

  <script>
    let lastScrollTop = 0;
    const banner = document.getElementById('top-banner');
    const nav = document.getElementById('main-nav');
    const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-to-top');
    const floatingCta = document.getElementById('floating-cta');

    window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
      let scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

      // Hide/Show banner on scroll
      if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
        banner.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
        nav.style.top = '0';
      } else {
        banner.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
        nav.style.top = '36px'';
      }

      lastScrollTop = scrollTop;

      // Show/Hide scroll to top & CTA
      if (scrollTop > 300) {
        scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
        floatingCta.classList.remove('hidden');
      } else {
        scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('hidden');
        floatingCta.classList.add('hidden');
      }
    });

    // Scroll to top functionality
    scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
      window.scrollTo({
        top: 0,
        behavior: 'smooth'
      });
    });
  </script>

    <script>
        // Mobile menu toggle
        const mobileMenuBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
        const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
        const menuIcon = document.getElementById('menu-icon');
        const mobileProductsToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-products-toggle');
        const mobileProductsMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-products-menu');

        mobileMenuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
          mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
          // Toggle icon between bars and times (X)
          if (mobileMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
            menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
            menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
          } else {
            menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-bars');
            menuIcon.classList.add('fa-times');
          }
        });

        mobileProductsToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
          mobileProductsMenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
        });

        // Close mobile menu when clicking on a link
        const mobileMenuLinks = mobileMenu.querySelectorAll('a');
        mobileMenuLinks.forEach(link => {
          link.addEventListener('click', () => {
            mobileMenu.classList.add('hidden');
            menuIcon.classList.remove('fa-times');
            menuIcon.classList.add('fa-bars');
          });
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        let lastScrollTop = 0;
        const banner = document.getElementById('top-banner');
        const nav = document.getElementById('main-nav');
        const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-to-top');
        const floatingCta = document.getElementById('floating-cta');
        
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            let scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
            
            // Hide/Show banner on scroll
            if (scrollTop > lastScrollTop && scrollTop > 100) {
                // Scrolling down
                banner.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
                nav.style.top = '0';
            } else {
                // Scrolling up
                banner.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                nav.style.top = '36px'';
            }
            
            lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
            
            // Show/Hide scroll to top button
            if (scrollTop > 300) {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
                floatingCta.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('hidden');
                floatingCta.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        });
        
        // Scroll to top functionality
        scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({
                top: 0,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        });
    </script>
